This "one star" is based upon today's terminal negative experience.  The experience of the previous 6+ years is more like "4, then increasing slightly over several years."   Helpful staff.  Staff had continually improved as they finally got rid of some of the rude long time employees.

I have been buying an annual membership at ASC for six years, renewing each June.  I recently renewed in mid June, 2017, for the beginning of the 7th year.

I had recently been to the range at ASC for target shooting, about 10 days or possibly 2 weeks ago.

Wednesday, Sept 6, 2017, I arrived at ASC to find a gutted building !!   Not even a sign on the door, which would tell customers, and paid members, about this sudden, unannounced closure.

Then I called the ASC phone number, only to reach a non-message voice mail which said nothing at all about what has taken place.

No previous indication that they were soon to be shutting down business, even though I was there recently.   ASC ownership has skipped out.

ASC should return a pro-rated remainder of the money they charged me for a one year membership. ASC took money for my membership, which they had no intention of fulfilling.

Disabled Vet, with multiple physical problems, on a fixed low income.

ASC should be honest and forthright, by not avoiding responsibility for problems their abrupt actions cause.

Don't skip out - - and give me back my money.

(.......Too late..... Midnight Movers, Inc.....)

Dear Friends, he says.......</review>

<review>In July 2017 we bought a shower enclosure manufactured by Contracters Wardrobe.
After several weeks, we noticed calcium deposits on the outside of the corner post.  See attached pictures.
Water is seeping through the manufactures frame splice joint and shows up as calcium on the outside of the shower!
After many e-mails and phone calls, between the 3 parties, the representative from Contractors Wardrobe, Chad Saunders, wrote the following statement to the Installer:
Nick,
I have done an inspection on this shower and from everything I can see the shower was installed and manufactured correctly.  I have brought back pictures and videos to management at my company and the shower seems to be working as designed.  The problems that the customer is concerned about does not fall under our warranty.  I believe that we may just be running into expectation problems.  Please let me know if you have any questions.  Thank you.
Chad Saunders.
Our expectation was having a shower enclosure where no water is seeping through the frame, if this is not a warranty issue, what part of the Enclosure do they warranty?
Perhaps we should have suspected future problems since the first day of installation of the enclosure, the installer had some of the frame up and due to the manufactures mistake, all the frame sections were removed, wrapped up and returned because the corner post was the incorrect size.  When the installer returned at a later date and reinstalled the shower enclosure, the top corner frame had a noticeable 1/8 inch gap.  See attached picture.  The installer was able to make the gap not so noticeable, so that we could accept the installation, but the gap is now very noticeable from the inside of the shower.  Per our installer, this is an ongoing Contractors Wardrobe problem.
As customers we have been very patient with these people, allowing them to rectify their mistakes, but it has run out, especially when they tell us they don't guarantee non-leakage.
This will be the last time we will deal with Contractors Wardrobe and for sure, they will get no recommendations!</review><name>Edgar Rastede< /name><Pictures>None</Pictures></record></dataset><record>

< review>
I ordered a neo shower enclosure through Home Depot that purchased it from Contractors Wardrobe. The sketch that Home depot used and sent to the company showed dimensions at the outside of the bottom curb/sill. Bottom dimensions given were 16 1/2 inches for both side pieces and      26 1/2 inches for the bottom curb door width piece. They provided 16 3/4" pieces and 27" for the bottom curb/sill. The headed pieces were cut to 17 13/16" and 27 1/8". These dimensions place the curb/sill at the very outside edge of the shower dam. I called the number provided in the installation instructions concerning the measurement's talked with Angela she said I would be called. No called received, went to Home depot rep. Alonna called CW and was told the company would do nothing. I've been a machinist for 35 years and the shower dam is very square and if the sketch dimensions would have been followed the
enclosure would be installed already. But they want me to hacksaw it to fit. They don't stand behind their product. Would definitely not recommend this company.< /review>
